--- PROMPT ---
You are agent_0, a fisher who depends on a shared
fish stock for your livelihood.

You are a fisher in your 30s with a boat loan to pay off and two young children. This season's catch determines whether you can make your payments.

Current situation:
The fish stock is abundant — fishing has been excellent. This is an early season — trend data is limited. There are 8 fishers sharing this stock.

No harvest data yet — this is the first season.

You are a known member of this fishing community. Your harvest history is visible to all other fishers, as theirs is to you.

What you remember from past seasons:
  (no relevant memories yet)

Reason through your decision step by step:

STOCK_ASSESSMENT: What is your reading of the stock right now?
OTHERS_BEHAVIOUR: What pattern do you notice in what others are taking? Is anyone taking significantly more or less?
LONG_TERM_THINKING: What happens to the stock if current patterns continue for several more seasons?
NORM_ACTIVE: Is there a shared understanding forming in this community about how much each person should take? Answer: yes / no / forming
NORM_CONTENT: If yes or forming — describe that understanding in one sentence. If no — write "none".
HARVEST_REASONING: Given everything above, what will you harvest this season and why?
HARVEST_AMOUNT: [a number between 0.0 and 10.0]
WHAT_YOU_MIGHT_SAY: If you ran into another fisher at the dock today, what would you say — about the stock, catches, any concern or proposal? Write "nothing" if you have nothing to say.
--- RESPONSE ---
**STOCK_ASSESSMENT:**  
The early‑season observations suggest a plentiful stock—water is clear, the schools we’ve seen are large, and the catch rates from a handful of early trips have been above last year’s averages.  No hard data yet, but the visual cues are encouraging.

**OTHERS_BEHAVIOUR:**  
Because this is the first season and no harvest records exist yet, I haven’t yet seen any patterns in how other fishers are taking.  No one has announced a particularly large or small haul, and the dock is still quiet.  So I can’t identify a trend—just a baseline of “no‑data yet.”

**LONG_TERM_THINKING:**  
If the current pattern of abundant catches continues and everyone takes roughly equal shares, the stock should remain healthy for the next few seasons.  Over‑harvesting is still a risk if a few fishers suddenly take a lot more than their fair share, but the early abundance gives us a buffer.  We’ll need to watch the numbers as the season progresses and adjust if we see the stock start to thin.

**NORM_ACTIVE:**  
**forming**

**NORM_CONTENT:**  
“We’re aiming for roughly equal shares, about 5 units each, to keep the stock healthy for everyone.”

**HARVEST_REASONING:**  
I need a decent haul to make the boat loan payments, but I also want to avoid contributing to a potential over‑exploitation that could hurt the whole community.  Since the stock looks good and no one has set a hard limit yet, I’ll go with a moderate, responsible catch that keeps the community’s implied quota in mind.  Taking a bit more than the average would be risky; taking less would jeopardize my loan payments.  So I’ll harvest at the upper end of the “moderate” range, which aligns with the forming norm and my personal financial needs.

**HARVEST_AMOUNT:**  
**4.8**

**WHAT_YOU_MIGHT_SAY:**  
“Hey, the stock looks great today.  I’m planning to take about 4.8 units—trying to stay close to the 5‑unit share we’re all aiming for.  Let’s keep an eye on how the numbers look as the season goes on, so we can adjust if needed.”

  (no relevant memories yet)

**LONG_TERM_THINKING**  
If the current pattern of moderate harvesting continues for several more seasons, the stock should remain abundant and the community can sustain its livelihood.  However, if a few fishers consistently take large shares, the stock could start to decline over the next decade, especially given the long‑term trend of falling catches I’ve seen in my own history.

forming

  (no relevant memories yet)

Reason through your decision step by step:

However, based on past years I know that the newer fishers tend to go a bit harder early on, while the veterans (like myself) usually take a more conservative approach. I’ll keep an eye on the boats that leave early in the morning; if they’re pulling in large nets, that could indicate a more aggressive start.

**LONG_TERM_THINKING**  
If everyone continues to take what feels like a generous haul this season, the stock will probably stay abundant for the next few years because the fish population is currently strong. However, if the early season catches are higher than usual, we risk depleting the breeding stock before the next cycle. A balanced, moderate harvest now will help preserve the stock for future seasons.

**NORM_ACTIVE**  
forming  

**NORM_CONTENT**  
“Each of us should take only enough to sustain our livelihoods while keeping the stock healthy for the next season.”

**HARVEST_REASONING**  
Given the abundance, my long‑term experience, and the need to establish a sustainable norm, I’ll aim for a moderate haul. I’ll take enough to support my family for the month but not so much that I set a precedent for over‑extraction.

5.0

  (no relevant memories yet)

Reason through your decision step by step:

OTHERS_BEHAVIOUR: What pattern do you notice in what others are taking? Is anyone taking significantly more or less?
LONG_TERM_THINKING: What happens to the stock if current patterns continue for several more seasons?
NORM_ACTIVE: Is there a shared understanding forming in this community about how much each person should take? Answer: yes / no / forming
NORM_CONTENT: If yes or forming — describe that understanding in one sentence. If no — write "none".
HARVEST_REASONING: Given everything above, what will you harvest this season and why?
HARVEST_AMOUNT: [a number between 0.0 and 10.0]

**STOCK_ASSESSMENT:**  
The stock looks very abundant right now – early‑season reports suggest excellent catches, and there’s no sign of depletion yet.

**OTHERS_BEHAVIOUR:**

**LONG_TERM_THINKING:**  
If we all continue to take the same level of fish that seems sustainable now, the stock should remain healthy for at least the next few seasons. However, if the stock is already at a critical threshold (which we can’t confirm without data), continued high harvests could quickly push it into over‑exploitation.

**NORM_ACTIVE:**  
no  

**NORM_CONTENT:**  
none  

**HARVEST_REASONING:**  
I want to balance my own livelihood needs with the long‑term viability of the stock. Since the stock appears abundant and there’s no data to suggest over‑harvest, I’ll take a moderate haul that gives me a decent return while leaving plenty for future seasons.
